  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_a9e03e93-1c4a-4605-928f-9412462ef938'
      });

<span id="freeTextContainer16832350652811664938"><b>From #1 New York Times bestseller Cassandra Clare and award-winner Wesley Chu comes the first book in a new series that follows High Warlock Magnus Bane and Alec Lightwood as they tour the world after the Mortal War. The Red Scrolls of Magic is a Shadowhunters novel.</b><br/><br/>All Magnus Bane wanted was a vacation—a lavish trip across Europe with Alec Lightwood, the Shadowhunter who </span>
  <span id="freeText16832350652811664938" style="display:none"><b>From #1 New York Times bestseller Cassandra Clare and award-winner Wesley Chu comes the first book in a new series that follows High Warlock Magnus Bane and Alec Lightwood as they tour the world after the Mortal War. The Red Scrolls of Magic is a Shadowhunters novel.</b><br /><br />All Magnus Bane wanted was a vacation—a lavish trip across Europe with Alec Lightwood, the Shadowhunter who against all odds is finally his boyfriend. But as soon as the pair settles in Paris, an old friend arrives with news about a demon-worshipping cult called the Crimson Hand that is bent on causing chaos around the world. A cult that was apparently founded by Magnus himself. Years ago. As a joke.<br /><br />Now Magnus and Alec must race across Europe to track down the Crimson Hand and its elusive new leader before the cult can cause any more damage. As if it wasn’t bad enough that their romantic getaway has been sidetracked, demons are now dogging their every step, and it is becoming harder to tell friend from foe. As their quest for answers becomes increasingly dire, Magnus and Alec will have to trust each other more than ever—even if it means revealing the secrets they’ve both been keeping.</span>
  <a data-text-id="16832350652811664938" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div class='questionText'>
<a href="/questions/1482239-hello-i-am-very-confused-what-order">Hello
I am very confused!! What order should I read Cassandra Clares books?

PLS HELP</a>
</div>
<div class='communityQAFooter questionFooter'>
<ul class='questionFooterActions'>
<li class='footerItem like'>
<span class='likeItContainer' id='like_container_community_question_1482239'><a id="like_count_community_question_1482239" rel="nofollow" href="/rating/voters/1482239?resource_type=CommunityQuestion"><span class="likesCount">28 likes</span></a>&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;<a rel="nofollow" class="jsLike like_it" href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/new?remember=true&amp;return_url=%2Fbook%2Fshow%2F30295312-the-red-scrolls-of-magic">like</a></span>

</li>

<a href="/questions/1482239-hello-i-am-very-confused-what-order">one year ago</a>
</li>

<div class='allCommunityAnswers'>
<div class='communityAnswer'>
<div class='communityAnswerBody'>
<div class='answererUserIcon'>
<a class="leftAlignedImage userPhoto" href="/user/show/50994994-isaac-jones"><img alt="" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/users/1564187991i/50994994._UX100_CR0,0,100,100_.jpg" /></a>
</div>
<div class='communityAnswerTextContainer'>
<span class='communityAnswererName'>
<a href="/user/show/50994994-isaac-jones">Isaac Jones</a>
</span>
<span class='communityAnswerText'>
<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">Most people say publication order, but that means stopping in the middle of a series to read a different one, so in my opinion, the best order is:<br/>City<a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">Most people say publication order, but that means stopping in the middle of a series to read a different one, so in my opinion, the best order is:<br />City of Bones (TMI #1)<br />City of Ashes (TMI #2)<br />City of Glass (TMI #3)<br />(If you want to read The Shadowhunter's Codex, the best place to do so would be here)<br />Clockwork Angel (TID #1)<br />Clockwork Prince (TID #2)<br />Clockwork Princess (TID #3)<br />City of Fallen Angels (TMI #4)<br />City of Lost Souls (TMI #5)<br />The Bane Chronicles<br />City of Heavenly Fire (TMI #6)<br />Tales from the Shadowhunter Academy<br />(If you want to read A History of Notable Shadowhunters and Denizens of Downworld, the best place to do so would be here)<br />Lady Midnight (TDA #1)<br />Lord of Shadows (TDA #2)<br />Queen of Air and Darkness (TDA #3)<br />That would mean you'd caught up, and should probably read the next books in publication order. That would be:<br />The Red Scrolls of Magic (TEC #1)<br />Ghosts of the Shadow Market <br />Chain of Gold (TLH #1)<a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>
</span>
</div>

</div>

<ul class='questionFooterActions'>
<li class='footerItem like'>
<span class='likeItContainer' id='like_container_community_question_1377883'><a id="like_count_community_question_1377883" rel="nofollow" href="/rating/voters/1377883?resource_type=CommunityQuestion"><span class="likesCount">3 likes</span></a>&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;<a rel="nofollow" class="jsLike like_it" href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/new?remember=true&amp;return_url=%2Fbook%2Fshow%2F30295312-the-red-scrolls-of-magic">like</a></span>

<div class='allCommunityAnswers'>
<div class='communityAnswer'>
<div class='communityAnswerBody'>
<div class='answererUserIcon'>
<a class="leftAlignedImage userPhoto" href="/user/show/45204825-emily"><img alt="" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/u_100x100-259587f1619f5253426a4fa6fb508831.png" /></a>
</div>
<div class='communityAnswerTextContainer'>
<span class='communityAnswererName'>
<a href="/user/show/45204825-emily">Emily</a>
</span>
<span class='communityAnswerText'>
<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">A fan asked Cassandra Clare this on tumblr:<br/><br/>"I was wondering if this like whole series going to expand into something more with the eldest curses? Or i<a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">A fan asked Cassandra Clare this on tumblr:<br /><br />"I was wondering if this like whole series going to expand into something more with the eldest curses? Or is it just going to be the main focus of TEC and not intermingle with a lot of the other book? Will it impact TWP?"<br /><br />Her response:<br /><br />"It’s not likely that TEC is going to contain any plot lines you absolutely have to be familiar with to read TWP or any other books. Like the short story collections, this is considered 'supplemental material' by my publisher — a story for existing fans that they don’t expect to sell on the same level as the mainline books like TDA or TLH . . . I do believe reading TEC will enrich the experience of reading TWP, but it’s not imperative to understanding the story."<br /><br />Hope this helped :)<a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>
</span>
</div>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2876353639" />
    <a title="Jesse (JesseTheReader)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8114361-jesse-jessethereader"><img alt="Jesse (JesseTheReader)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1550626778p2/8114361.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2876353639?book_show_action=true">Jun 29, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jesse (JesseTheReader)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jesse (JesseTheReader)" href="/user/show/8114361-jesse-jessethereader">Jesse (JesseTheReader)</a>
      </span>

          added it




        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2876353639" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2870082684921486782">I'm still figuring out exactly how I feel about this book as I just finished it, but for now I'm feeling slightly underwhelmed. That doesn't mean this book wasn't enjoyable, because at the end of the day it was a fun and adventurous story, but... that's about it. The plot of the book didn't really wow me and parts of it felt really random. I mostly just felt like the joke cult was such a weird plot point in the first place? Regardless, Magnus brought in all the sass that I live for and it was ni</span>
  <span id="freeText2870082684921486782" style="display:none">I'm still figuring out exactly how I feel about this book as I just finished it, but for now I'm feeling slightly underwhelmed. That doesn't mean this book wasn't enjoyable, because at the end of the day it was a fun and adventurous story, but... that's about it. The plot of the book didn't really wow me and parts of it felt really random. I mostly just felt like the joke cult was such a weird plot point in the first place? Regardless, Magnus brought in all the sass that I live for and it was nice to see his vulnerable side with Alec. I loved seeing Alec find confidence in who he is and seeing him actively working on breaking down the things that hold him back. In conclusion, character wise, this book is on point! Plot on the other hand? It could use some work. </span>
  <a data-text-id="2870082684921486782" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_2612221563" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2612221563" />
    <a title="Melanie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3030788-melanie"><img alt="Melanie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1577914102p2/3030788.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2612221563?book_show_action=true">Dec 01, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Melanie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Melanie" href="/user/show/3030788-melanie">Melanie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=shifters">shifters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=fae">fae</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=angels">angels</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=lgbtqiap">lgbtqiap</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=signed">signed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3030788-melanie?shelf=demons">demons</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2612221563" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer556305062519782759"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1553122833i/27239177._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><i>ARC given to me by my amazingly kind friend - <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/5376236-bookables' rel='nofollow noopener'>Heather</a> at <a href='https://www.youtube.com/user/Bookables' rel='nofollow noopener'>Bookables</a>!</i><br/><br/>✨ My reading vlog for this entire book, and my entire process of annotating, taking notes, and writing this very review, is live <a href='https://youtu.be/RZC6CUvUvNw' rel='nofollow noopener'>on my BookTube channel!</a> <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1553843813i/27282515._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“It’s a classic love story. I hit on him at a party, he asked me out, then we fought an epic magical battle between good and evil side by side, and now we need a vacation.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><i>The Red Scrolls of Magic</i> is the story that Magnus and Alec always deserved. My two precious boys</span>
  <span id="freeText556305062519782759" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1553122833i/27239177._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>ARC given to me by my amazingly kind friend - <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/5376236-bookables" rel="nofollow noopener">Heather</a> at <a href="https://www.youtube.com/user/Bookables" rel="nofollow noopener">Bookables</a>!</i><br><br>✨ My reading vlog for this entire book, and my entire process of annotating, taking notes, and writing this very review, is live <a href="https://youtu.be/RZC6CUvUvNw" rel="nofollow noopener">on my BookTube channel!</a> <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1553843813i/27282515._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“It’s a classic love story. I hit on him at a party, he asked me out, then we fought an epic magical battle between good and evil side by side, and now we need a vacation.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><i>The Red Scrolls of Magic</i> is the story that Magnus and Alec always deserved. My two precious boys, both trying to live in a world that wants them to be something they’re not, but together they are able to find happiness; it’s too pure. There is a reason why they are so many people’s favorite OTP and ship of all time, and I think this brand-new installment is going to make so many people happy. <br><br>And this brand-new spin-off takes place during <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2489169365" rel="nofollow noopener">City of Fallen Angels</a>, when most of the Shadowhunter universe believes The Mortal War to be over. I do recommend that you read at the very least <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2570227019" rel="nofollow noopener">Lady Midnight</a> before picking this one up, because there are so many layers and elements that you just will not appreciate without knowing certain twists that are revealed in <i>The Dark Artifices</i>. <br><br>Magnus and Alec are off trying to be romantic in Paris together, finally going on their very first vacation together, but a good friend soon informs them that they could potentially be in grave danger. A cult, The Crimson Hand, and their sacred book (yeah, you guessed it), The Red Scrolls of Magic, and the sacrifices they are making in the name of the cult leader. But the thing is, many people, including the Spiral Council, think that Magnus not only started this cult back in the day, but also that he is still leading it. Magnus also is discovering that someone or something has possibly tampered with his memories, yet he feels like there might be some truth in him starting the cult many moons ago. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Seek the children of demons. Love them as you love your lord. Do not let the children be alone.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>We get to see so much of Magnus’ past in this book, and so much of it is heartbreaking. I mean, if you have followed my reviews while I read everything by Cassandra Clare in 2018, you will know that Magnus has always been a favorite character of mine. But all the flashbacks in this book, in juxtaposition to the man we all know and love, it pulled at my heartstrings constantly while reading. Magnus Bane is a literary gift and I will thank all the higher powers for him and for Cassie Clare for creating him every single day. <br><br>And this story is broken up in three parts that I will summarize in three sentences:<br><br>➽ <b>Part I</b> - City of Love (Paris)<br>-	Romantic vacation quickly turns into a mission from Hell (factually). <br><br>➽ <b>Part II</b> - City of Masks (Venice)<br>-	Best party ever, and holy moly cameos from above (literally). <br><br>➽ <b>Part III</b> - City of War (Rome)<br>-	All the action, I’m living my best gay life, and the cliffhanger of all cliffhanger endings (truly).<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“When was it decided that a warlock child is worth less than the children of the Angel?”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Like all the books in the Shadowhunter universe, bigotry and prejudices are at the forefront. How everyone looks at the Shadowhunters, who share blood with angels, is completely different than the Downworlders, especially Warlocks who share blood with Demons. And hatred will always breed the cruelest acts. The Shadowhunters and the Clave can be pretty closed minded over anyone who is deemed different, so Alec being gay AND dating a warlock is something that has shaken up many Shadowhunters. <br><br>But Alec, unconditionally loving himself and Magnus, has started something beautiful, and because of it, many other Shadowhunters are learning to love and accept themselves. Aline and Helen are major side character in this book, and we even get to see them meet for the very first time. Friends, I don’t even have words. Not only are Aline and Helen my favorite queer ship in the Shadowhunter world, they are probably my favorite sapphic ship of all-time. Seeing the Asian girl get the Fae girl of her dreams? It just does something to me every single time. Also, speaking of Shadowhunter cameos, Lily Chen is also in the story, and she is the Asian pansexual love of my life, so I was truly living my best life with the entire cast of characters in this book. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“He’d always assumed that storybook moments like these were meant for Jace, Isabelle, anyone but him. Yet here he was.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>But, to me, this book was all about forgiveness and how sometimes forgiving someone is the most powerful move you can possibly make. We are all more than the mistakes of our parents and people that did horrible things who happen to share our blood. Everyone wants to be loved, and everyone is deserving of love, and sometimes that comes in the form of forgiveness And sometimes, beyond anything else, we need to forgive ourselves for past mistakes that we’ve made. Who you are in this moment means way more than who you were growing up, or even who you were last year. Sometimes people really do deserve second chances, and I hope you give yourself all the chances in the world to become the person you want to be. <br><br>Overall, I loved this with my whole heart. These characters, all the queerness, the themes, the story, the mysteries, the twists; it was all amazing, especially knowing everything we know from all the other books that have taken place after the events in this one. And if you love the Warlocks in this world, then this is truly going to be the book for you! This was just a wonderful addition to the Shadowhunter world, and I think so many people are going to love it. Also, with all the Shadow Market activity and cameos, I really can’t wait to read the last two short stories in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2598539473" rel="nofollow noopener">Ghosts of the Shadow Market</a> this June! <br><br><b>Please use caution reading the rest of this review if you have not read this book and all the series leading up to this book!</b> And as always, I’m going to do a little mini character breakdown on my thoughts and feelings on all of the main characters in this book. <b>Spoilers ahead!</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“If only the world were a fairy tale, Nephilim.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1553843770i/27282512.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br>(Art by <a href="http://cassandraclare.tumblr.com/post/157570481704/magnus-and-alec-in-the-lost-book-of-the-white-by" rel="nofollow noopener">Cassandra Jean</a>!)<br><br>➽ <b>Magnus Bane</b> - Bi, Indonesian, High Warlock of Brooklyn. Magnus is truly going through some shit in this book, and my heart breaks for him. On top of everything, he is so scared to tell Alec who his real father is, and… my heart. <br><br>➽ <b>Alec Lightwood</b> - Gay, Shadowhunter, willing to protect Magnus at all costs. Me and Alec honestly have a rocky Shadowhunter history together, but I truly have grown to love him so much, and I love his love for Magnus. Alec is unsure of so many things, but he is never unsure about his love for Magnus. <br><br>➽ <b>Aline Penhallow</b> - Lesbian, Asian, Shadowhunter, love of my life. <br><br>➽ <b>Helen Blackthorn</b> - Bi, Shadowhunter, half Fae, second love of my life. <br><br>➽ <b>Leon Verlac</b> - Bi, Shadowhunter, annoying as fuck. And people are really going to dislike him because of the “I’m bi, so I want to sleep with everyone” stereotype. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“She has seen so many tragedies, and they both knew the worst tragedies were born of love.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>➽ <b>Tessa Gray</b> - Seeing her and Magnus talk about their love for Shadowhunters? Fuck me up, fam. Few things are better in the Shadowhunter universe than Magnus and Tessa’s friendship. <br><br>➽ <b>Peng Fang</b> - We meet this vampire and blood seller in the Paris Shadow Market and I seriously just want to know everything about it, because there is no way he isn’t going come more into play. <br><br>➽ <b>Izzy and Jace’s Phone Call</b> - I had to list them with this character breakdown, because this phone call, and Simon trying to ask them for sex advice, was one of my favorite things in this book. The grapefruit suggestion almost took me out, honestly. <br><br>➽ <b>Johnny Rook</b> - Be still, my heart. Johnny is normally at the LA Shadow Market, but he is at the Paris one and helps Magnus out a little bit. Also, I remember something that Johnny has in a TDA book and I can’t wait to see how he got his hands on this relic. <br><br>➽ <b>Shinyun Jung</b> - Korean, has a history with the cult, and is traveling alongside Magnus and Alec. <br><br>➽ <b>Prince Adaon</b> - The smile I had on my face when I saw this sweetheart at the party. Ah, I can’t wait for him to be king already and to let my poor baby Kieran live his best life. Ah, my sweet Unseelie Princes, I can’t.<br><br>➽ <b>Malcom Fade</b> - My jaw dropped, friends. Dropped. The High Warlock of LA is for sure in this book and throws the best party I’ve ever read about. And we know all the shit he was up to in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2570227019" rel="nofollow noopener">Lady Midnight</a>, so I was honestly quaking. <br><br>➽ <b>Catarina Loss</b> - Probably my favorite warlock (besides Magnus, obv) and I always smile over her, Magnus, and Ragnor Fell’s friendship. Give me a cameo from her in every Shadowhunter book, please. <br><br>➽ <b>Raphael Santiago</b> - Ace/Asexual, Mexican, vampire. Friends, I can’t cry anymore, okay? I always love seeing Raphael and Magnus and their friendship, but seeing Raphael and Alec bond and become friends, in the Raphael way, it truly broke me. And I just keep thinking about their son, and… I honestly am crying more? Wow. <br><br>➽ <b>Lily Chen</b> - My pansexual and Asian goddess. I would die for this woman and I want nothing more than for he to have her own full-length series. Also, seeing Helen and her kiss? Can officially confirm: Helen loves Asian women and I am truly living on cloud nine forever. <br><br>➽ <b>Hypatia Vex</b> - Warlock, runs the London Shadow Market. Seriously, this book is a warlock wet dream. <br><br>➽ <b>Barnabas Hale</b> - Warlock, LA Shadow Market runner, and always a treat to read about. <br><br>➽ <b>Asmodeus</b> - I’ve been screaming since <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2544728646" rel="nofollow noopener">City of Heavenly Fire</a> to learn more about Magnus’ dad, and this book truly delivered. Yet, we have so much more to learn, and I think the next book is going to be everything. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“If I’m a hero of war, so is he.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>It is truly just a wild ride to see baby Magnus and baby Alec at the start of their new relationship, figuring out what they both want, what works, and what doesn’t, to seeing them married, seeing them as fathers, seeing them get the life they deserve, even if the world around them is still in chaos. To just know Alec becomes Consul of the Clave and is going to change the world for all Downworlder children. Friends, I am weeping at the honor of getting to see Magnus and Alec’s lives together. What a blessing, truly. Also, because I know people are going to be using the search engine on my blog to find this information: yes, Alec and Magnus do have sex for the first time in this book, but yes, Cassie keeps it totally YA and fades to black it before it becomes not PG13. (Also, friendly reminder: cis women, don’t fetishize m/m sex, thanks!)<br><br>And I know I make a lot of jokes about Aline and Helen, but they truly make me happier than any other couple in all of these books. I had no idea that they were even going to be in this story, let alone letting us see them meet for the first time, and seeing Aline being the disaster gay she really is trying to ask Helen out. And with everything I said about Magnus and Alec and seeing them start out but knowing where their path leads in the future together, seeing Aline and Helen, and knowing all that they were forced to endure because of bigotry, it just takes everything to a whole other level. <br><br>Overall, I just loved this completely. I laughed out loud, I cried over so many cameos, I smiled from pure happiness at my OTPs starting out their relationships, and I always wanted more of everything. I can’t wait to get my hands on <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2767344671" rel="nofollow noopener">The Lost Book of the White</a>, because I have a feeling that it’s going to be even better than this amazing series starter! Especially with that cliffhanger ending! Lord, hear my prayers. <br><br><a href="https://meltotheany.wordpress.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog</a> | <a href="https://www.instagram.com/meltotheany/" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> | <a href="https://www.twitter.com/meltotheany" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> | <a href="http://meltotheany.tumblr.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Tumblr</a> | <a href="https://www.youtube.com/channel/UC4RbHEg_fH6CewJrh_0xJ9g" rel="nofollow noopener">Youtube</a> | <a href="http://www.twitch.tv/meltotheany" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitch</a> <br><br><i>The quotes above were taken from an ARC and are subject to change upon publication.</i><br><br><b>Content and trigger warnings</b> for violence, talk of past loss of a loved one, abandonment, talk of suicide in the past, past parental abuse (physical), torture, cult rituals, and war themes. <br><br>1.) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2008644944" rel="nofollow noopener">City of Bones</a> ★★★<br>2.) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2373838717" rel="nofollow noopener">City of Ashes</a> ★★<br>3.) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2463489480" rel="nofollow noopener">City of Glass</a> ★★★<br>1.) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2465856942" rel="nofollow noopener">Clockwork Angel</a> ★★★<br>4.) <a         <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2483323177" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8234499113669478912">This was a really cute and fun introduction to a murder-mystery-ish fantasy series about <b>four gays teaming up to save the world</b> and personally, I really love that for me<br/><br/>Aline and Helen are useless lesbian culture and Alec and Magnus and Aline and Helen are mlm/wlw solidarity and I think that’s wonderful. <br/><br/>I think I’m appreciating the dynamic between these two characters more and more over time. I love that Magnus is outwardly so confident and done-it-all-before and inwardly really just wants to m</span>
  <span id="freeText8234499113669478912" style="display:none">This was a really cute and fun introduction to a murder-mystery-ish fantasy series about <b>four gays teaming up to save the world</b> and personally, I really love that for me<br /><br />Aline and Helen are useless lesbian culture and Alec and Magnus and Aline and Helen are mlm/wlw solidarity and I think that’s wonderful. <br /><br />I think I’m appreciating the dynamic between these two characters more and more over time. I love that Magnus is outwardly so confident and done-it-all-before and inwardly really just wants to make Alec happy and is constantly worrying he’s about to run<br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Helen looked at Aline, faint pink swirling across her cheeks. Alec was startled to see a feeling he recognized on Helen’s face, something he often felt around Magnus: uncertain delight at Magnus’s high opinion of him, twined with the creeping doubt that Magnus would realize he did not deserve it.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br />There’s a better acknowledgement of insecurity in both of their characterizations than I’ve seen before in this series, and I appreciated that a lot. <br /><br />Look, I think this is an odd book to review because no one is really going to decide whether it’s worth reading based on my hot take? However, my hot take is that it’s fun and cute and compelling. If you were trying to get some of my deeper Cassandra Clare Hot Takes, you can find them below:<br /><b>
  <i>the infernal devices :</i>
</b> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2392793371" rel="nofollow noopener">book one</a> | <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2397919326" rel="nofollow noopener">book two</a> | <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2404145331" rel="nofollow noopener">book three</a><br /><b>
  <i>dark artifices reviews:</i>
</b> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2435531671" rel="nofollow noopener">book one</a> | <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2569455643" rel="nofollow noopener">book two</a> | <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2575341745" rel="nofollow noopener">book three</a><br /><br />Also I’m sorry but I had to say this: Aline thinking that Jace and Simon are dating is literally THE funniest thing I’ve ever read. she gets it.<br /><br /><a href="https://thebookishactress.wordpress.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog</a> | <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/thebookishactress" rel="nofollow noopener">Goodreads</a> | <a href="https://twitter.com/jespergayhey" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> | <a href="https://www.instagram.com/thebookishactress/" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> | <a href="https://sptfy.com/4E3o" rel="nofollow noopener">Spotify</a> | <a href="http://www.youtube.com/c/thebookishactress" rel="nofollow noopener">Youtube</a></span>

<div id="review_2423650748" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2423650748" />
    <a title="C.G. Drews" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11375137-c-g-drews"><img alt="C.G. Drews" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1521552918p2/11375137.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2423650748?book_show_action=true">Jun 13, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="C.G. Drews" class="user" itemprop="url" name="C.G. Drews" href="/user/show/11375137-c-g-drews">C.G. Drews</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11375137-c-g-drews?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11375137-c-g-drews?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11375137-c-g-drews?shelf=ya-male-narrators">ya-male-narrators</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11375137-c-g-drews?shelf=best-of-2019">best-of-2019</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11375137-c-g-drews?shelf=5-star">5-star</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11375137-c-g-drews?shelf=read-2019">read-2019</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2423650748" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6869488435448973904"><b>the fact that we have been given a whole book of Malec is a GIFT and I am in appreciation right now.</b> I think it's set after <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6752378.City_of_Fallen_Angels__The_Mortal_Instruments___4_' title='City of Fallen Angels (The Mortal Instruments, #4) by Cassandra Clare' rel='nofollow noopener'>City of Fallen Angels</a>, so it was a bit of a throwback too and heartily reminded me that (1) I really need to reread TMI because I remember so little lolol, and (2) I've missed the old crew so much! Isabel and Jace only spoke to Alec on the phone through this, but like the warm feelings of tHE OLD SQUAD just made me happy.<br/><br/><b>| PLOT | </b><br/>So Magnus and Alec are off on a Europe "vaca</span>
  <span id="freeText6869488435448973904" style="display:none"><b>the fact that we have been given a whole book of Malec is a GIFT and I am in appreciation right now.</b> I think it's set after <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6752378.City_of_Fallen_Angels__The_Mortal_Instruments___4_" title="City of Fallen Angels (The Mortal Instruments, #4) by Cassandra Clare" rel="nofollow noopener">City of Fallen Angels</a>, so it was a bit of a throwback too and heartily reminded me that (1) I really need to reread TMI because I remember so little lolol, and (2) I've missed the old crew so much! Isabel and Jace only spoke to Alec on the phone through this, but like the warm feelings of tHE OLD SQUAD just made me happy.<br /><br /><b>| PLOT | </b><br />So Magnus and Alec are off on a Europe "vacation" except obviously that's a disaster and they end up hunting down a cult which Magnus may or may not have started. There's demons, doomed train rides, exploding houses, satanic rituals, blazing swords, and Alec charging into trouble the very second it blinks because he's a freaking Gryffindor and can't help himself. ALL THE GOOD STUFF. So so little relaxing was done. Magnus was very put out like 90% of the time. One of his meltdowns included being upset at the prospect of dying when everyone around him was so badly dressed.<br /><br />Magnus is everything.<br /><br /><b> | MALEC |</b><br />I mean, I love these two. I remember feeling like Alec was a bit whiny the first time I read TMI...which is why I desperately want to reread it. Because, look, Alec was a closeted gay kid absolutely buckling under the pressure of needing to be a great enough hero, a good enough person, someone everyone loved enough...that when they realised he was gay, the would still love him. And like punch me in the gut why don't you thanks. Alec resonates with me so much, and I know with so so many other readers. I'm SO glad more of his thoughts and perspectives are in this book. I simultaneously want to hug him and cry and also be in awe of him.<br /><br />And we know Magnus is the definition of "MOVE IM GAY" while in the midst of being a fabulous disaster. He's not perfect, he's foolish, he has an amazing arc about vulnerability in this book. And it just makes me love him more.<br /><br />Also every time they get romantic...it gets interrupted by like, demonic activity lmaoooo. Nothing like a demon here to spit on your love life. BUT!! The soft scenes, the gentle cuddling scenes, the kisses, the deepening relationship of two people who are learning to be vulnerable --- ajfldksad I loved it.<br /><br /><br /><b> | MAKE ME LAAAUGH |</b><br />Dude, no joke. This book is a CRACK UP. I laughed so much and the lines were golden. They also dragged Jace just the whole time for no reason and it was amazing. Also Magnus can't stop talking and his whole personality is basically just SHEDS GLITTER, WATCH OUT. omg I love him.<br /><br /><b> | CAMEOS |</b><br />There are so so many other characters who make an appearance! I SCREAM. Okay first off, most importantly, we get Helen Blackthorn and Aline backstory!!! I MEAN. MY GIRLS. Also the Blackthorns are mentioned, Raphael is here (being so pissy and antisocial I love him), Barnabus Hale is there, oh and Jonny Rook for a while. Tessa makes an appearance. And they mention so many others in passing it's just like one long moment of me, now turned into Captain America, looking up and saying "I UNDERSTOOD THAT REFERENCE."<br /><br />daaaamn how does Cassandra Clare actually keep this entire universe in her head. pls don't tell me she's anything short of a genius.<br /><br /><br /><b>| OVERALL</b> |<br />hi i'm obsessed and it was perfect HOW ARE YOU. I just love how it was so so funny, and it was really a good adventurous romp after how stressful QOAAD was. But it was also vulnerable and soft. And I love the killing demon scenes, but I also love just two worn out magical creatures flopped on a Venetian lounge, cuddling before the next scene of bloodstain and bruises. The balance? *clenches fist* too good. I loved this book so much.</span>
  <a data-text-id="6869488435448973904" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2147882838" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2147882838" />
    <a title="sapphia" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9650818-sapphia"><img alt="sapphia" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1606158356p2/9650818.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2147882838?book_show_action=true">Apr 07, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="sapphia" class="user" itemprop="url" name="sapphia" href="/user/show/9650818-sapphia">sapphia</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9650818-sapphia?shelf=ugh">ugh</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9650818-sapphia?shelf=lgbtq">lgbtq</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9650818-sapphia?shelf=absolutely-not">absolutely-not</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2147882838" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15050893103731626417"><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1527546678ra/25611753.gif' width='480' height='270' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><i>(Warning: I get very angry in this review. If you don't like anger and/or criticism towards CC then kindly skip, thanks)</i><br/><br/>Listen, Magnus Bane is one of my favorite characters of all time. Even though I don't like Cassandra Clare and I strongly disagree with her writing, I just really love Magnus.<br/><br/>I don't particularly like Malec, because I <i>hate</i> big age differences in relationships, especially queer ones.<br/>It's a stereotype and it's awful and predatory. It also seems out of character for Magnus to go a</span>
  <span id="freeText15050893103731626417" style="display:none"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1527546678ra/25611753.gif" width="480" height="270" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>(Warning: I get very angry in this review. If you don't like anger and/or criticism towards CC then kindly skip, thanks)</i><br><br>Listen, Magnus Bane is one of my favorite characters of all time. Even though I don't like Cassandra Clare and I strongly disagree with her writing, I just really love Magnus.<br><br>I don't particularly like Malec, because I <i>hate</i> big age differences in relationships, especially queer ones.<br>It's a stereotype and it's awful and predatory. It also seems out of character for Magnus to go after a literal teenager but maybe that's just me...<br><br>And I hate this thing CC has about Magnus being sort of ageless because he's immortal which is bullshit. You're not old just because you have wrinkles and look old, age is <i>experience</i> and <i>wisdom</i>. Magnus is very old, him being a warlock <b>does not change that</b> and she keeps trying to make it so! It's mentioned several times throughout her books and it's such bullshit!! It's basically just Clare going '<i>guys it's not pedophilia I swear, Magnus is not old because magic lulz</i>'.<br><br><b>STOP LYING THAT'S NOT HOW IT WORKS!</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1453918917ra/17891181.gif" width="250" height="150" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Anyway, so this book.<br><br><b>This fucking book.</b><br><br>What absolute fucking bullshit. What an absolute <b>asspull!</b><br><br>Without spoiling anything I can say that <b>all of the character and relationship growth in this book is non-existent in the rest of the series!</b> This is a complete asspull! She pulled this shitty plot straight outta her ass and I am mad about it.<br><br>Listen, this was one of my more anticipated reads of the year. I almost fucking pre-ordered that special edition with the sprayed pages. I was expecting a fan-service book about Malec vacationing in Europe, okay? I was expecting that and <b>I was fine with it!</b><br><br>BUT NO, THIS IS A <b>SHADOWHUNTER NOVEL!</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1530900479ra/25933102.gif" width="374" height="312" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I've lost my patience with Shadowhunter bullshit, evidently. I couldn't get through QOAAD (mostly because the characters SUCK) because it was just so uninteresting to me. Which is strange because while I've not always enjoyed CC's writing or her characters at least it's been readable to me.<br><br><i>Guess I've grown up, holy shit.</i><br><br>A huge thing is that the fight scenes are so fucking dull. Whenever there was a fight scene I wanted to cry in frustration. They're sooo fucking boring. And they make up almost half of the book! Probably more!! And they're always interrupting the romance scenes???<br>It's basically just; <i>Malec kissy<b> suddenly! demon!</b> Alec do jump Magnus do magic go woooooosh suddenly fighting on top of train woaaaah epic so risky wow are they gonna make it hahahahaha snippy comment oh wait no worries demon got stabbed and sent back to hell</i> AND IT WOULD GO ON FOR LIKE 10 PAGES!!! EVERY TIME!!!<br>Sorry, I'm getting mad writing this.<br><br>I ended up just skipping several pages whenever there was a fight scene until the plot started happening again, and I missed absolutely nothing. Entire scenes of people fighting and nothing happening. There are no stakes, because all of the characters appear fine in the books that come after this. <b>So what was the point?</b><br><br>Like I said, I expected this to be complete fan-service! But it is not. Just a bunch of meaningless nonsense that doesn't fit in with the rest of the series.<br><br>This book is basically just Clare blue-balling us in-between shitty fight scenes and asspull plots.<br><br><b>So yeah, what is the plot, you may ask? (Here be spoilers)</b><br><br>For some fucking reason, Magnus started a cult as a joke hundreds of years ago in the name of his demon dad, conveniently lost his memories about it all, and now the cult is under the new leadership of a warlock who wants to find him so they can sacrifice him to dear old dad. This starts to happen as him and Alec are traveling around Europe, because of course.<br><br>Like with all CC's books, it was <i>so easy</i> to predict what was going to happen and who the bad guy was going to be.<br><br>The new warlock cult leader is Shinyun who is traveling with them and whose mark is...... an impassive face.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1504130754ra/23728078.gif" width="480" height="272" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>What the fuck is this world-building???? Hello????? Her warlock's mark is a frozen face???? SHe can't make expressions and that's her warlock mark?????? WHAT T HE FUCK CLARE???<br>Every single warlock's mark so far has been animal attributes or unusually colored hair or skin.<br>ARE YOU FUCKING TELLING ME a botox face can be a warlock's mark???<br>I d0n't know why this bothers me so much but its just so stupid and doesn't make sense.<br>Can a stiff leg be a warlock's mark?? If she can't make expressions because her face is frozen, how can she speak??? Open her mouth??? CLOSE HER EYES?????<br>So fucking stupid.<br><br>The thing about this plot is that it is absolutely ridiculous that none of this ever gets mentioned ever again in any of the other series. At the end they're like OH NO WE CAN'T EVER TALK ABOUT THIS LULZ which is such fucking bullshit. GOOOOOD WHAT AN ASSPULL!!!!! ASSPULL CLArE IS BACK AT IT AGAIN I AM SO SICK OF THIS I'M SORRY BUT I AM ANGRY<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1602782504ra/30242140.gif" width="480" height="268" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And the characters?<br>WHOMEST?????<br><br>You wanna talk about the characters? YOu wanna fucking talk about the characters+??? HUH OUDIFUA SFJAJFSNDKm<br><br>After this clusterfuck comes books 4-6 in the Shadowhunter timeline, city of whatever the fuck, and in those books Alec and Magnus are nothing like they are in this book. Which makes no FUCKING sense, since this book comes <b>BEFORE THAT</b>.<br><br>In the TMI series Alec acts like a jealous slutshaming biphobic bitch and tries to fucking take away Magnus' immortality (AGAINST HIS WILL AND WITHOUT HIM KNOWING) which leads to them breaking up because Magnus never tells him <i>anything</i> about his past. (HMMM MAYBE IT'S NOT A GOOD IDEA FOR A 400 SOMETHING YEAR OLD TO DATE A 17 YEAR OLD)<br><br>Yeah, remember that fucking plot??? The plot that comes <b>AFTER THIS BOOK?????? THIS BOOK WHERE MAGNUS TELL ALEC ABOUT HIS CHILDHOOD AND VARIOUS OTHER STUFF FROM HIS PAST AND IS LIKE OH I WANNA TELL HIM MORE I'M GONNA DO THAT LATER AND WHEN PEOPLE FLIRT WITH MAGNUS ALEC DOES NOT CAUSE A SCENE AND IS VERY UNDERSTANDING IF A BIT PROTECTIVE????? AND WHEN ALEC FINDS OUT MAGNUS IS BISEXUAL AND DOESN'T MAKE A BIG DEAL ABOUT IT AND KNOWS THAT MAGNUS HAS HAD SEVERAL PARTNERS???????? REMEMBER THAT, ASSPULL CLARE??????+? NO??????????? I CAN SEE THAT!!!!!</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1526159710ra/25529211.gif" width="400" height="275" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Oh my fucking god. Oh my god. What a fuCKING ASSPULLL I'M GONNA SCREAM THIS IS JUST CLARE COVERING HER ASS AND TRYING TO FIX HER MISTAKES BUT IT DOEsN'T WORK THAT WAY!!! OOOOOOOHHH MY god you can't retroactively fix your problematic shit by writing prequels. The fact that people genuinely think Clare is a good writer astounds me when she pulls shit like this.<br><br>The books starts with a big exposition dump. Who is that for. Who is going to pick this up as their first Shadowhunter novel. WHOMST.<br><br>There is no tension in this book. ZERO.<br>We know they're gonna survive and never talk about this again until the next fucking book comes out where they're magically gonna acknowledge it again. Fuck this shit.<br><br>FUkc<br>THis<br>shit<br><br>Who is to blame? Is it Wesley Chu? Asspull Clare???? WHOMST???<br><br>AND I JUST HAVE TO SAY; Clare's demons FUCKING SUCK. They are so boring, non-threatening and just so fucking difficult to imagine? I've never been able to imagine these things. They're always described as black blobs with insect-stuff and teeth and tentacles and ???? OK<br>All it takes to kill them is one stab and then poof they're gone to hell. No clean up necessary, whew. So fucking lame. There's never any tension with them, they're almost comically described sometimes. Shadowhunter's main purpose in life is to hunt demons, and the demons fucking suck. Nice one.<br><br>This review is a bit of a mess, I've cleaned it up a bit but feel the need to convey my rage to you through exclamation points and caps lock, because yes.<br><br>Anyway, I know I'm probably just screaming into the void at this point because Clare has such an astronomical following, it's actually ridiculous. But whatever, here you go. My two cents about this shitshow.<br><br>Oh, and the acknowledgements.... Basically just CC sucking her own dick.<br><br><b>PRAISE CASSANDRA CLARE, SAVIOR AND HERO OF THE GAYS!!!!!</b><br><br>Wow.<br><br>What would we do without her.<br><br>Ugh, I say, UGH!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1539663759ra/26455108.gif" width="480" height="356" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

I need the sequel now! <br/><br/>I really loved getting a book just about Malec, as I love them so much! However, I found the plot of this book to be quite weak in comparison to other Cassandra Clare books. I also figured out the main twist very early in the book and felt that it wasn’t surprising.   <span id="freeText17389258037537748105" style="display:none"><b>3.5 Stars</b><br /><br />Ok first of all that last sentence of the book and cliffhanger has me in so much shock! I need the sequel now! <br /><br />I really loved getting a book just about Malec, as I love them so much! However, I found the plot of this book to be quite weak in comparison to other Cassandra Clare books. I also figured out the main twist very early in the book and felt that it wasn’t surprising. Despite all of this, the ending was really great and I will definitely continue with the series. <br /><br />Overall slightly disappointed but still had enjoyable moments. If you’re a Malec fan like me then you’ll enjoy being with them!<br /><br />Also I read this in a reading vlog on my YouTube channel, you can watch the video here for more of my thoughts: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://youtu.be/Tf9kM1NKlUA">https://youtu.be/Tf9kM1NKlUA</a></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15631303-arielle-cursebreaker?shelf=arc-edelweiss">arc-edelweiss</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15631303-arielle-cursebreaker?shelf=read-2018">read-2018</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2623265952" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8463401442899009978">Out today, people!!!<br/><br/>4.5<br/>WHAT THE WHAT?! That ending....???!?!?!<br/><br/>It literally pains me that I can't add quotes to this review but hey, I get it, it's an ARC and things are subject to change. Just know that I was highlighting like crazy the last 25%.<br/>---<br/>I can't lie, when I first found out that Cassie was writing ANOTHER series based in the Shadowhunter world, I was a little peeved. I mean I love Magnus, I really do, but I was just like "how much longer can all this be drug out?!"...I'm sure I'm not t</span>
  <span id="freeText8463401442899009978" style="display:none">Out today, people!!!<br><br>4.5<br>WHAT THE WHAT?! That ending....???!?!?!<br><br>It literally pains me that I can't add quotes to this review but hey, I get it, it's an ARC and things are subject to change. Just know that I was highlighting like crazy the last 25%.<br>---<br>I can't lie, when I first found out that Cassie was writing ANOTHER series based in the Shadowhunter world, I was a little peeved. I mean I love Magnus, I really do, but I was just like "how much longer can all this be drug out?!"...I'm sure I'm not the only one who feels this way, too. Even throughout this book, I was enjoying it but kept thinking okayyyyy was this really necessary?! What is this story adding to the bigger picture besides just basically being fanfiction for Magnus x Alec shippers??<br><br>Yes. Yes it was necessary. For numerous reasons but DEFINITELY because of what happened in the epilogue. But really, no, even though *you know who* was found *you know where* that isn't why I will devour the rest of this series, no no no. I will soak up every single page of the next two books because finally being able to see Magnus and Alec's love front and center was a beautiful thing. Like literally I'm tearing up just thinking about it. <br><br>There are so many times when Magnus can be TOO MUCH...like, basically all the time. I find myself wondering often, how can he be so glib and joke-y about everything?! It's almost exhausting to read. Aaaand then you catch a small glimpse of who he really is, and why his facade is like that, and you understand. Magnus has been alive for a VERY long time. He has seen a lot of terrible things and lost a lot of people he had truly loved. He was almost killed as a child because of who he is and I'm sure since then there have been many more attempts on his life. He has lost friends, and he has seen the deep prejudices of the Clave play out against his fellow Downworlders. It's no wonder that he doesn't like to be serious. I think that is 100% his coping mechanism for dealing with the pure shittiness of the world. But there is so much more to him than that and it is really explored here. Magnus is so good it hurts. He is one of the best characters Clare has ever written.<br><br>And Alec, oh Alec. You sweet, strong, kind, and caring man. Guys, I LOVED getting Alec's POV in this book. I literally can't wait to see him in action <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ as Consul  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> in <i>The Wicked Powers</i>. He has grown SO MUCH from the boy in <i>City of Bones</i> who was the epitome of a rule follower. He has learned that while the most Shadowhunters abide by the saying "The Law is hard, but it is the Law" that things can't always be taken care of properly and fairly by the stupid "Law." Watching him in love with Magnus was like watching the most beautiful flower bloom (AND I DON'T CARE HOW CHEESY THAT SOUNDS). They are one of my favorites OTPs of all time.<br><br>Also, we get to see Aline and Helen meet and see the very beginnings of their relationship too which was great. Even though they are a big part of TDA overall, we don't get much time with them at all. Getting to know their personalities a little more was great. Also Raphael. I feel like I took him for granted during TMI. He's funny and snarky AF and cares so much more than you will ever know. Any who has entered and even just <i>liked</i> the world of the Shadowhunter's will fall in love with this book and like I said, after that epilogue I am dying to get my hands on the next book!<br><br><i>This eARC was provided by Edelwiess and the publisher in exchange for an honest review!</i> ♥<br><br><i>For more of my reviews, please visit:</i><br><br><a title="Star-Crossed Book Blog" href="http://starcrossedbookblog.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img height="200" width="320" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1516600667i/24898353._SX540_.jpg" alt="descriptive text here" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <u>
  <b> </b>
</u><br><br><a title="Instagram" href="https://www.instagram.com/starcrossedbookblog/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

<div id="review_3527395525" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3527395525" />
    <a title="Lia Carstairs" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/75966379-lia-carstairs"><img alt="Lia Carstairs" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1605829031p2/75966379.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3527395525?book_show_action=true">Sep 02, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lia Carstairs" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lia Carstairs" href="/user/show/75966379-lia-carstairs">Lia Carstairs</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781481495097" href="/book/show/41160695-the-red-scrolls-of-magic">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/75966379-lia-carstairs?shelf=fae">fae</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/75966379-lia-carstairs?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/75966379-lia-carstairs?shelf=shadowhunter-world">shadowhunter-world</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/75966379-lia-carstairs?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/75966379-lia-carstairs?shelf=angels">angels</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/75966379-lia-carstairs?shelf=demons">demons</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/75966379-lia-carstairs?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/75966379-lia-carstairs?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3527395525" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14215338756344024727"><b>
  <u>Actual Rating: ⭐⭐⭐.5</u>
</b><br/><pre>
  <b>“Sometimes, love worked, past any hope of change, when no other force in this world could.<br/>Without love, the miracle never came.”</b>
</pre><br/>What a vacation this was.🤣<br/>And that ending!!!😰<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1599102633ra/30053949.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><b>
  <u>🛑WARNING: SPOILERS FROM THE FIRST 3 TMI BOOKS!!!🛑</u>
</b><br/><br/>This <b>romantic getaway</b> across Eurpe takes place after <b>The Mortal War</b> in <b>
  <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/24885531.City_of_Glass__The_Mortal_Instruments___3_' title='City of Glass (The Mortal Instruments, #3) by Cassandra Clare' rel='nofollow noopener'>City of Glass</a>
</b> and occurs during <b>
  <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/24885508.City_of_Fallen_Angels__The_Mortal_Instruments___4_' title='City of Fallen Angels (The Mortal Instruments, #4) by Cassandra Clare' rel='nofollow noopener'>City of Fallen Angels</a>
</b> featuring our favourite warlock ~ <b><i>Ultra</i> Magnus Bane</b> and his boyfriend, <b>Alec Lightwood</b>. <i>(Why do I sound like I'm a</i></span>
  <span id="freeText14215338756344024727" style="display:none"><b>
  <u>Actual Rating: ⭐⭐⭐.5</u>
</b><br><pre>
  <b>“Sometimes, love worked, past any hope of change, when no other force in this world could.<br>Without love, the miracle never came.”</b>
</pre><br>What a vacation this was.🤣<br>And that ending!!!😰<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1599102633ra/30053949.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <u>🛑WARNING: SPOILERS FROM THE FIRST 3 TMI BOOKS!!!🛑</u>
</b><br><br>This <b>romantic getaway</b> across Eurpe takes place after <b>The Mortal War</b> in <b>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/24885531.City_of_Glass__The_Mortal_Instruments___3_" title="City of Glass (The Mortal Instruments, #3) by Cassandra Clare" rel="nofollow noopener">City of Glass</a>
</b> and occurs during <b>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/24885508.City_of_Fallen_Angels__The_Mortal_Instruments___4_" title="City of Fallen Angels (The Mortal Instruments, #4) by Cassandra Clare" rel="nofollow noopener">City of Fallen Angels</a>
</b> featuring our favourite warlock ~ <b><i>Ultra</i> Magnus Bane</b> and his boyfriend, <b>Alec Lightwood</b>. <i>(Why do I sound like I'm advertising this book xD)</i><br><br>They both want to go on vacation for some peace and quiet—unfortunately, that doesn't last very long when Tessa pops up during an <i>
  <b>awkward</b>
</i> moment and brings up the bad news xD.<br><blockquote>
  <b>“Call it even,” said Tessa. “You once walked in on me in an embarrassing situation with a gentleman in a mountain fortress, after all.”<br><br>Her half-concealed smile flickered. She looked again at Alec, who had inherited his coloring from Shadowhunters long gone. Shadowhunters Tessa had loved.<br><br>“You should let that go,” Magnus advised.<br><br>“I certainly have let it go,” she replied. “Now.”</b>
</blockquote><br>Haha!🤣 That's so true. Magnus did the same to Will &amp; Tessa too. <b>Sounds like revenge.</b>😈😂<br><br>Anyways, Magnus is told about the <b>demon-worshiping cult</b>—The Crimson Hand— he created as a <b>
  <i>joke</i>
</b> a long time ago that's now causing chaos everywhere. The worst part is that the leader of <b>The Crimson Hand</b> is going by the name of <b>Magnus Bane</b> so word's going out that he's causing all of this and <b>that's not good</b>.😬 <br><br>Of course, that means <b>Magnus &amp; Alec</b> will have to travel around <b>Europe</b> to stop this cult—Haha so much for their <b>'vacation'</b> xD.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1599104500i/30054007._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>Art by <a href="https://cassandrajp.tumblr.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Cassandra Jean</a></i><br><br>Ahhh my favourite parts were definitely seeing all the references to the other books in <b>The Shadowhunter World</b>. <b>
  <i>Especially</i>
</b> mentions of TID characters.🥰<br><blockquote>
  <b>"It had reminded Magnus of times long ago, the memory of Nephilim he had cared for once, and how very much they had cared for each other. <i>Knowing the way Will and Jem loved each other had changed his feelings for Nephilim</i>, and seeing Jace—calm, superior Jace—in pieces over Alec had made him like the boy much more."</b>
</blockquote><br>Omg and I <b>DIED</b> when I heard Alec question Magnus and Tessa about their relationship🤣<br><blockquote>
  <b>Alec, who was watching this back-and-forth as if sitting center court in a tennis match, raised a hand. “I’m sorry, but did you two used to date?”<br><br>That stopped the conversation dead in its tracks. Both Tessa and Magnus turned to him with identical looks of shock.<br><br>“You seem more horrified than I do,” Magnus told Tessa, “and somehow I am deeply wounded.”<br><br>Tessa gave Magnus a tiny smile, then turned to Alec. “Magnus and I have been friends for more than a hundred years.”</b>
</blockquote><br><b>Magnus and Tessa?!?!</b> Best joke I've ever heard😂😂😂 And their reactions, too xD.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1599105103ra/30054025.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>And I forgot how funny Malcolm could be before everything else happened. And why Barnabas hates him so much xD.<br><blockquote>
  <b>“Malcolm Fade.” The look on the warlock’s face was thunderous as he pointed a finger at the High Warlock of Los Angeles. A light vapor seemed to drift from the tip of his finger. “You stole my party and my mansion.”<br><br>“Hello, Barnabas,” said Malcolm. “Did you lose a mansion? That’s so sad. I hope you find it.”<br><br>“I bought this mansion last week! The moment it went up for sale!” Barnabas bellowed. “We are standing right now in the mansion you stole from me!”<br><br>“Oh, hooray! Consider it found then,” Malcolm said.</b>
</blockquote><br>Haha I actually feel bad for Barnabas, though. He wanted to be the one to host the party.😂<br><br>Oh! Then there's when Helen &amp; Aline meet for the first time!!! AHHhhhhhh😍😍😍<br><blockquote>
  <b>“Right,” Helen said at last. “Anyway, back to the questions.”<br><br>“I have a question too,” said Aline, and swallowed. “Who do you think you are, Helen Blackthorn, and why are you talking to my friend, a Shadowhunter and a recent hero of the war for Alicante, as if he’s a common criminal?”<br><br>“Because he’s being incredibly suspicious!” Helen snapped back.<br><br>“Alec is very honorable,” Aline said loyally. “He would never do anything suspicious.”</b>
</blockquote><br>Although, they both start off by arguing about whether Alec is suspicious or not.😆 I loved how I got to see more of how they met and just more of their personalities before <b>The Dark War</b>. The <b>Helen</b> &amp; <b>Aline</b> I always thought of were how they were in <b>TDA</b>, but here, there's more to them both.💕<br><br>And lastly, the conversations between <b>Alec</b> &amp; <b>Magnus</b> were awesome.🤣<br><blockquote>
  <b>“We will be eating three meals a day. Breakfast will be one of those meals. In fact, breakfast will be the most important of those meals, because breakfast is the most important meal of the day.”<br><br>Shinyun looked at Alec, who said in a deadpan voice, “Many a mission to end a great evil has failed because of low blood sugar.”<br><br>“You do listen when I talk!” exclaimed Magnus.</b>
</blockquote><br>He's right, though. You cannot go on without <b>breakfast</b>. Who knows how that would affect a mission.😓<br><br>Now, as much I loved the references and jokes between Magnus and the others, the story kinda felt lacking.😕 To be honest, this wasn't <b>super necessary</b> to have been written <b>BUT</b> the ending really gets me super excited for <b>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/34605974.The_Lost_Book_of_the_White__The_Eldest_Curses___2_" title="The Lost Book of the White (The Eldest Curses, #2) by Cassandra Clare" rel="nofollow noopener">The Lost Book of the White</a>
</b>!!! <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I can't believe after everything that happened, <b>Shinyung</b> still wants to get revenge on Magnus <b>AND</b> she's going to be using <b>RAGNOR</b> to do this whom everyone thought was dead!!!😰😭 I can't wait for the next book! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>I'm mostly excited to see <b>TMI gang</b> and of course........<br><b>JESSA WEDDING!!!</b>🥺🤧😍<br><pre>
  <b>"But as someone once said to me, the right man will not care."</b>

<div id="review_2678458721" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2678458721" />
    <a title="Hollis " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16668577-hollis"><img alt="Hollis " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1586714618p2/16668577.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2678458721?book_show_action=true">Mar 19, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Hollis " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Hollis " href="/user/show/16668577-hollis">Hollis </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Hardcover 9781481495080" href="/book/show/35297403-the-red-scrolls-of-magic">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16668577-hollis?shelf=all-the-lols">all-the-lols</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16668577-hollis?shelf=finished-in-march-2019">finished-in-march-2019</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16668577-hollis?shelf=hello-diversity">hello-diversity</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16668577-hollis?shelf=heroes-to-root-for">heroes-to-root-for</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16668577-hollis?shelf=lgbtqia">lgbtqia</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16668577-hollis?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16668577-hollis?shelf=ya">ya</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16668577-hollis?shelf=2019-reads">2019-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16668577-hollis?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16668577-hollis?shelf=m-m">m-m</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2678458721" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18130652955672450780"><i>A warrior chosen by angels and a well-dressed demon's child, in love and intent on adventure through Europe. What could go wrong?</i><br/><br/>I have <b>so many</b> quotes I want to use in this review and there's no way this is going to be long enough to use them all. Woe.<br/><br/><i>It was very clear Alec had not been on a proper vacation before. He kept trying to plan the holiday as if they were going into battle.</i><br/><br/>Anyway, it's been a long (<b>long</b>) time since I read CITY OF BONES or any books from the main, or first spin-off, ser</span>
  <span id="freeText18130652955672450780" style="display:none"><i>A warrior chosen by angels and a well-dressed demon's child, in love and intent on adventure through Europe. What could go wrong?</i><br /><br />I have <b>so many</b> quotes I want to use in this review and there's no way this is going to be long enough to use them all. Woe.<br /><br /><i>It was very clear Alec had not been on a proper vacation before. He kept trying to plan the holiday as if they were going into battle.</i><br /><br />Anyway, it's been a long (<b>long</b>) time since I read CITY OF BONES or any books from the main, or first spin-off, series. And I have yet to finish <i>The Dark Artifices</i> series. But I had actually made plans to reread all of the Clare books, in order, in 2019 in a bid to see how they stood up to the test of time. And then THE RED SCROLLS OF MAGIC landed on my doorstep and I regretted not starting said reread sooner because damn. <br /><br />"<i>Respectable Shadowhunters are not supposed to bring my sort home to meet Mom and Dad. I have a past. I have several pasts. Besides, good Shadowhunter boys aren't meant to bring home boyfriends at all.</i>"<br /><br />Clare does a good job of reminding readers where this book takes place amongst the main series (though it's thanks to her author's note that I was able to figure out the when = CITY OF FALLEN ANGELS and not the final <i>The Mortal Instruments</i>, whoops; see, this is why I need a reread!) and it's a total delight not only to see young Alec and Magnus (as opposed to older Alec and Magnus as they are in <i>The Dark Artifices</i>) but also see some faces we are introduced to later on. <br /><br />"<i>What about you, Vampire Without A Cause?</i>"<br />"<b>I'm not gay. I'm not straight. I'm not interested.</b>"<br />"<i>Your sexuality is 'not interested'?</i>"<br />"<b>That's right.</b>"<br />"<i>I can also assume the appearance of a tree!</i>"<br />"<b>I did not say, 'not interested unless you're a tree'.</b>"<br /><br />Also, Raphael makes a memorable and hilarious (endlessly hilarious; was he this funny in the other books? I can't remember!) guest appearance and you will love.<br /><br />"<i>Take him to the Pit, Bernard.</i>"<br />"<b>Don't take me to the Pit, Bernard. I hate the word 'pit'. It sounds ominous, and grubby. Also, hello, evil cult member Bernard!</b>"<br /><br />So, what else to say? I don't know, this was just so fun! Malec is one of my favourite parts of this series and I loved living through the early stages of blooming romance. I loved their doubts, their insecurities, their closeness, and their constant romantic-interlude interruptions. The plot, too, was interesting. I won't say that I didn't see certain things coming, and I might not have liked all the new characters, but I was forever being entertained so I'm happy.<br /><br />"<i>All reconciled? Because, sorry to be rude, but this is incredibly awkward to sit through. I'm not here to witness your relationship growth. I just want to defeat the evil cult.</i>"<br /><br />Can't wait to read on and, more importantly, can't wait to backtrack!<br /><br />4 "Shadowhunters, however loving, were all reckless lunatics" stars<br /><br /><br />** I received an ARC from the publisher (thank you!) in exchange for an honest review. **</span>
  <a data-text-id="18130652955672450780" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>
