    <a title="kav (xreadingsolacex)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/54570527-kav-xreadingsolacex"><img alt="kav (xreadingsolacex)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1585981757p2/54570527.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2163233636?book_show_action=true">Mar 30, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="kav (xreadingsolacex)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="kav (xreadingsolacex)" href="/user/show/54570527-kav-xreadingsolacex">kav (xreadingsolacex)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/54570527-kav-xreadingsolacex?shelf=young-adult-fantasy">young-adult-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/54570527-kav-xreadingsolacex?shelf=bad-bitches">bad-bitches</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/54570527-kav-xreadingsolacex?shelf=disaster-mcs">disaster-mcs</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/54570527-kav-xreadingsolacex?shelf=stories-of-hope">stories-of-hope</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/54570527-kav-xreadingsolacex?shelf=queer-fiction">queer-fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/54570527-kav-xreadingsolacex?shelf=superior-writing-style">superior-writing-style</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/54570527-kav-xreadingsolacex?shelf=all-time-favorites">all-time-favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/54570527-kav-xreadingsolacex?shelf=asian-fiction">asian-fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/54570527-kav-xreadingsolacex?shelf=found-family">found-family</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2163233636" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8566997988361723398"><b>
  <i>disclaimer: i received an ARC from the publisher in exchange for an honest review, this is no way impacted my review</i>
</b><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Alec had been right about the darkness waiting in Magnus, and the pain waiting with it. All that darkness, and all that pain, and Magnus was somehow still a blazing riot of life and color, a source of joy for everyone around him. He was the reason Alec looked a mirror now and saw a complete person who did not have to hide.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><br/><i>The Red Scrolls of Magic</i> by Cassandra Clare </span>
  <span id="freeText8566997988361723398" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>disclaimer: i received an ARC from the publisher in exchange for an honest review, this is no way impacted my review</i>
</b><br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Alec had been right about the darkness waiting in Magnus, and the pain waiting with it. All that darkness, and all that pain, and Magnus was somehow still a blazing riot of life and color, a source of joy for everyone around him. He was the reason Alec looked a mirror now and saw a complete person who did not have to hide.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br /><br /><i>The Red Scrolls of Magic</i> by Cassandra Clare and Wesley Chu is the latest installment in <i>The Shadowhunter Chronicles</i>, the first of a series that follows the story of Alexander Lightwood and Magnus Bane, the single most valid relationship. This first novel takes place during Alec and Magnus' vacation in <i>City of Fallen Angels</i>, carting us and the two men in love around Europe.<br /><br />This novel is beyond exquisite.<br /><br />This novel allows for the exploration of a kind of relationship that almost never gets time to a shine in literature - a queer biracial couple. Alec, a gay shadowhunter, and Magnus, a bisexual Southeast Asian warlock, are the heroes of this novel.<br /><br />So much of this story is dedicated to furthering their relationship and allowing it to flourish in the most beautiful way possible. There is something so special to having watched the growth of a relationship from their beginning all the way to their current status.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Alec always believed in the Law, but if the Law didn't shield Magnus, the Law should be changed.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br /><br />Also, the character depth and exploration is magnificent. Magnus is one of very few characters who has been in every shadowhunter novel to-date, and yet, due to his immortality and mysterious past, there is always more to explore with his character. Then, there's Alec, who is possibly the Clare character that I would argue has had the most monumental growth of all of them. Many readers may give that title to Jace, but I firmly believe it belongs to Alec.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Telling the truth makes me happy...Magnus makes me happy. I don't care if it's difficult."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br /><br />LOOK. AT. THAT. CHARACTER. DEVELOPMENT. A gay man in a homophobic society learning to love himself for his sexuality and his entire self and standing up to the people who tell him to hide his truth??? YES PLEASE.<br /><br />Then, there is also the added bonus that so many familiar faces show up over the course of this novel. I am not going to point all of them out, but I am going to point out my favorite four.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"I'm not gay," said Raphael. "I'm not straight. I'm not interested."<br />"Your sexuality is 'not interested'?" Alec asked curiously.<br />Raphael said, "That's right."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Yeah you're gonna have to be more specific than that," said the vampire woman. "This is a party. I've made out with six faerie girls, four faerie boys, and a talking toadstool whose gender I'm unsure about. Pretty sexy for a toadstool, though."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Helen looked at Aline. Faint pink stole in her cheeks. Alec was startled to see a feeling he recognized on Helen's face, something he often felt around Magnus: uncertain delight at Magnus' high opinion of him, twined with the creeping doubt that Magnus would realize he did not deserve it.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br /><br />This book is so <b>
  <i>unapologetically queer,</i>
</b> and though I did not know it when I first discovered this world, quite a few of my favorites in this world are those queer members who make cameos in this book.<br /><br />From the angsty Latino aro/ace vampire Raphael Santiago, to the flamboyant pansexual Asian vampire Lily Chen, and the budding romance of one of the most iconic sapphic ships including the dedicated bisexual half-faeire half-Shadowhunter Helen Blackthorn and the completely loyal Asian lesbian Aline Penhallow, Clare and Chu really allow the reader to dig into all ends of the queer spectrum.<br /><br /><i>(Sidenote: these characters were also just so hilarious I could not breathe.)</i><br /><br />But in doing so, they do not forget about the people of color.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Go back to where you came from," murmured a man in Italian, glancing from Magnus' Indonesian to Shinyun's Korean face.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br /><br />This line gave me chills. The subliminal way in which Clare always includes social commentary on the bigotry existent within our world, often within the shadowhunter world but here it is within <b>our world</b>, is one of the most profoundly moving parts of her writing for me as a reader.<br /><br />But outside of representation and character development, Clare and Chu also include an action-packed, suspenseful plot that truly keeps the reader on the edge of their seat. In traditional Cassie Clare, the villainous reveal is an absolute mind-fuck, so I do not want to comment too much on this as I feel it is far better to experience it yourself.<br /><br />Cassandra Clare just has a way of making every reader feel so invested in every single character she brings to life, and <i>The Red Scrolls of Magic</i> just further confirms her talent as a writer and allows for further exploration into a brilliantly created fictional world with some of the best characters to ever exist.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"I've realized-I don't need to change. And neither do you, Helen, or you, Aline. It's the world that needs to change. and we're going to be the ones to change it."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote></span>
  <a data-text-id="8566997988361723398" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2864411162" />
    <a title="Sol ~ TheBookishKing" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/69919640-sol-thebookishking"><img alt="Sol ~ TheBookishKing" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1596427937p2/69919640.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2864411162?book_show_action=true">Jun 19, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sol ~ TheBookishKing" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sol ~ TheBookishKing" href="/user/show/69919640-sol-thebookishking">Sol ~ TheBookishKing</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Hardcover 9781481495080" href="/book/show/35297403-the-red-scrolls-of-magic">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/69919640-sol-thebookishking?shelf=cute">cute</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/69919640-sol-thebookishking?shelf=cover-lovin">cover-lovin</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/69919640-sol-thebookishking?shelf=better-than-food">better-than-food</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/69919640-sol-thebookishking?shelf=lgbtqiap">lgbtqiap</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2864411162" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7149553726918150010"><i>“If only the world were a fairy tale, Nephilim.”</i><br/><br/> <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1561620290i/27732276._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='300' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I have finally got around to my most anticipated release of 2019 and it really didn’t disappoint! After the disaster that is Queen of Air and Darkness, I was really scared to read this but this reminded me of the Cassie Clare that I’ve loved all along.<br/><br/><b>Spoiler Free Overview</b><br/>This book takes place I believe during City of Fallen Angels, but definitely after the war in City of Glass. It’s been so long since I’ve read The Mortal Instruments I’m not exac</span>
  <span id="freeText7149553726918150010" style="display:none"><i>“If only the world were a fairy tale, Nephilim.”</i><br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1561620290i/27732276._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I have finally got around to my most anticipated release of 2019 and it really didn’t disappoint! After the disaster that is Queen of Air and Darkness, I was really scared to read this but this reminded me of the Cassie Clare that I’ve loved all along.<br><br><b>Spoiler Free Overview</b><br>This book takes place I believe during City of Fallen Angels, but definitely after the war in City of Glass. It’s been so long since I’ve read The Mortal Instruments I’m not exactly sure the perfect timeline. BUT anyways, Red Scrolls of Magic is about Alex and Magnus on their first trip out of the country to the beautiful Paris. It’s supposed to be a nice relaxing vacation after the events of the war and of course, nothing goes as it’s supposed to in a Cassie Clare book. While on vacation a cult becomes rowdy and a favorite character of all ours seems to be attached to them. So forget the beautifully romantic vacation that they had planned, and now a mystery is stirring and both Alec and Magnus’ life could be on the line.<br><br>I never once felt bored while reading this book and as someone who has been a Malec Stan for well over five years, I loved every second. There are so many sweet moments between the two that I was tabbing away at the book and ended up almost using a whole sheet. It is so wonderful to find out more about Magnus’ past and how he came to be his spectacular sparkly self. And it was also great to see more into Alec’s head and how he deals with his sexuality while growing up in such a constricting society. Alec is someone I’ve always looked to see myself in and I actually managed to grow to love him more in this book (I truly didn’t think this was possible.) Getting to experience the events that brought them closer and closer truly just punched me right in the heart. Overall, seeing their relationship grow and flourish was beautiful and I couldn’t be happier.<br><br><i>“He knew what he had done and what he had fought for, and he knew what he would fight for in the future. And he knew exactly who he loved.”</i><br><br>Cassie and Wesley managed to mix sexiness, wittiness, and great on your toes action very well. This reminded me so much of the Shadowhunter Stories I fell in love with when I was younger. It was so incredibly exciting to see some old favorites of mine again even if it did make me a little emotional. Years later, having to read about JemWillTessa makes me tear up and I hate it but OH WELL. I seriously cannot wait to see what they do with the rest of this series and who else will make a reappearance.<br><br>Now, I will say definitely hold off on reading this until you’ve finished reading The Dark Artifices Trilogy. There isn’t a lot of spoilers for that series, or any spoilers really. But you do meet some characters from TDA that are introduced in that trilogy and it just makes for a better experience if you wait to read those three books first.<br><br>This is a great installment to the Shadowhunter Chronicles and this really made me want to just dive in and reread all of Cassies’ Books. But honestly, no one has the time for that lol.<br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="7149553726918150010" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_2780568668" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2780568668" />
    <a title="Emma" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/32710668-emma"><img alt="Emma" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1579952193p2/32710668.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2780568668?book_show_action=true">Apr 13, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Emma" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Emma" href="/user/show/32710668-emma">Emma</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2780568668" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3890792463529203112">3.75 stars<br/><br/>Full review <a href='https://booksrealwhenshared.wordpress.com/2019/04/20/the-red-scrolls-of-magic-by-cassandra-clare-wesley-chu-review/' rel='nofollow noopener'>here</a><br/><br/>I must say that I enjoyed this book a lot more than I had expected. I’m not gonna lie, I wasn’t very excited about this book, just because it’s set in the recent past and so I already know that they’re going to be fine and nothing major is going to happen to them. But I was pleasantly surprised because I found it enjoyable and also because I think this book laid the ground for the next two in the series. <br/><br/>Alec and Magnus are very cute and I enjoyed reading about their re</span>
  <span id="freeText3890792463529203112" style="display:none">3.75 stars<br /><br />Full review <a href="https://booksrealwhenshared.wordpress.com/2019/04/20/the-red-scrolls-of-magic-by-cassandra-clare-wesley-chu-review/" rel="nofollow noopener">here</a><br /><br />I must say that I enjoyed this book a lot more than I had expected. I’m not gonna lie, I wasn’t very excited about this book, just because it’s set in the recent past and so I already know that they’re going to be fine and nothing major is going to happen to them. But I was pleasantly surprised because I found it enjoyable and also because I think this book laid the ground for the next two in the series. <br /><br />Alec and Magnus are very cute and I enjoyed reading about their relationship. I love Magnus for being himself and always trying to amaze Alec, who in the end only really wants one simple thing, Magnus’s love. Their love really shines in this book, something that I think was overlooked in the original TMI series. <br />Another lovely surprise were Aline and Helen. I’m a big fan of the two of them and it was so nice to see them meet and fall head over heels in love with each other from day one basically. <br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ I can’t wait to see what the deal with Ragnor Fell is. It was not explained in the last book from TDA and so now I’m really curious to learn more.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></span>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('YtrSwyqxgCCRHuLpCNLqeJKS3JCSZ0v80tRpMVO/9n80IlDo5laN68D/zqst/4A4noaeks0gS2vMkdWRxJfI6w==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('lcpAt0BfdQoVFzOhX9fWkTSxEr2njydADsQggebbE67DMsKcjLh4wUT2H+N6+rzROKVQv/jIJ9cQgZwhcfMtOg==')})
  }
//]]>

  <span id="freeText14958515045270561599" style="display:none">Hello Goodreadsers. Here's my official bio:<br /><br />"Cassandra Clare was born overseas and spent her early years traveling around the world with her family and several trunks of fantasy books. Cassandra worked for several years as an entertainment journalist for the Hollywood Reporter before turning her attention to fiction. She is the author of City of Bones, the first book in the Mortal Instruments trilogy and a New York Times bestseller. Cassandra lives with her fiance and their two cats in Massachusetts."<br /><br />You can find me online at <br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.cassandraclare.com">www.cassandraclare.com</a><br /><br />I have a blog:<br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://cassandraclare.livejournal.com/">http://cassandraclare.livejournal.com/</a><br /><br />and a Facebook:<br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.facebook.com/Cassandraclare">http://www.facebook.com/Cassandraclare</a><br /><br />and a Twitter:<br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.twitter.com/cassieclare">www.twitter.com/cassieclare</a><br /><br />I'll be available here on Goodreads to answer questions for a Goodreads Author Discussion starting September 18 — <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/37113.Q_A_with_Cassandra_Clare">http://www.goodreads.com/group/show/3...</a><br /><br />Go sign up so you don't miss the conversation when it starts!</span>
